### FRENCH

# Principes :
# L'écriture de la commande: Get + chaîne au masculin avec majuscule + chaîne au féminin avec majuscule
# Ajouter Cap à la fin pour avoir une majuscule dans le texte cible
# Ajouter Opp pour inverser le masculin et le féminin
# L'apostrophe pour les élisions n'est pas représenté dans le nom des commandes
# Le paramètre "fallback_text" permet d'avoir une ligne de localisation utilisée au cas où aucune condition n'est remplie, en l'occurrence la commande anglaise correspondante.

# GetIlElle
# GetIlElleCap

## COMMANDE ACCOLEE A UNE COMMANDE OU UN MOT (PAS D'ESPACE ENTRE LES DEUX)
# Get_only_du_RealmFull (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_en_RealmFull (dans le\dans la\dans l'\chez les devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_le_RealmFull (le\la\l'\les devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_au_RealmFull (AuAlaAux devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_du_Realm (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetName) *TITLE
# Get_only_le_Realm (le\la\l'\les devant GetName) *TITLE
# Get_only_en_Realm (en\dans le\dans la\dans l'\dans les\chez les devant GetName) *TITLE
# Get_only_du_Title (du\de la\de l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_le_Title (le\la\l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_Le_Title (Le\La\L' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_au_Title (au\à la\à l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_Au_Title (Au\À la\À l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_e_Title (e\' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_du_Society (du\de la\de l'\des devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_le_Society (le\la\l'\les devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_Le_Society (Le\La\L'\Les devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_au_Society (au\à la\à l'\aux devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_le_SocietyRank (le\la\l' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_Le_SocietyRank (Le\La\L' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_au_SocietyRank (au\à la\à l'\aux devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_du_SocietyRank (du\de la\de l' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_e_SocietyRank (e\' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_le_JobTitle (le\la\l' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_Le_JobTitle (Le\La\L' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_du_JobTitle (du\de la\de l' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_au_JobTitle (au\à la\à l' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_on_JobTitle (on\a devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_e_JobTitle (e\' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_du_SelectedIngredient_1 (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_du_SelectedIngredient_2 (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_le_SelectedIngredient_1 (le\la\l'\les devant GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_le_SelectedIngredient_2 (le\la\l'\les devant GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_e_SelectedIngredient_1 (e\' devant GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_e_SelectedIngredient_2 (e\' devant GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_du_HighGod (du\de la\de l' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_au_HighGod (au\à la\à l' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_le_HighGod (le\la\l' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_Le_HighGod (Le\La\L' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_du_HighGodTrue (du\de la\de l' devant TrueReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_au_HighGodTrue (au\à la\à l' devant TrueReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_le_HighGodTrue (le\la\l' devant TrueReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_du_HighGodSecret (du\de la\de l' devant SecretReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_le_Scripture (le\la\l'\les devant Religion.GetScriptureName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_du_Scripture (du\de la\de l'\des devant Religion.GetScriptureName) *RELIGION

defined_text = {
	name = GetIlElle
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetIlElle_male
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetIlElle_female
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

defined_text = { # 2018.10.30
	name = Get_only_du_Title
	use_first_valid = yes
	text = { # Titre temporaire non nommé (en révolte, aventurier, ordre sacré)
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_
		trigger = { 
			primary_title = { temporary = yes }
		}
	}
	text = { # titres honorifiques
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = { 
			AND = { # Prince, Rajkumar, Shahzada, César
				has_minor_title = title_prince
				is_female = no
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { 
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					trait = bastard # non si bâtard
					spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = DUKE } # non si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { # titres honorifiques
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_la_
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				AND = { # Kaiserin
					has_minor_title = title_queen_mother
					culture = german
				}
				AND = { # Princesse, Rajkumari, Shahdokht, Caesarina
					has_minor_title = title_prince
					is_female = yes
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { 
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						trait = bastard # non si bâtard
						spouse = { # non si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
							AND = {
								higher_tier_than = DUKE
								primary_title = { temporary = no }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { # titres honorifiques
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_l
		trigger = { 
			has_minor_title = title_queen_mother # Impératrice douairière
			NOT = { culture = german } # Kaiseri
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = { # homme qui contrôle une religion
			is_female = no
			controls_religion = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_la_
		trigger = { # femme qui contrôle une religion
			is_female = yes
			controls_religion = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = { # homme avec un titre spécial
			is_female = no
			primary_title = {
				OR = {
					title = e_sunni # CALIPH Calife
					title = e_shiite # CALIPH Calife
					title = d_papal_guards # CAPTAIN Capitaine
					title = d_sunni_turkic_company # CAPTAIN Capitaine

								culture = saxon # Earl

							NOT = {

								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = BARON
							is_female = no
							culture_group = iranian # Argbadh
							NOT = { spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON } } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						}
						AND = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
								NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
									culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
									culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
									culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
									culture = nahuatl # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

									culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin

									culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine

									AND = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
										OR = {
											culture = turkish # Padishah
											culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
											culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										}
										is_female = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Exarque)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = KING
							}
							spouse = {
								tier = KING
								primary_title = { is_vice_royalty = yes }
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = byzantine

									liege = { culture_group = byzantine }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = DUKE

								real_tier = COUNT

							is_female = no

								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes

					}
				}

					is_theocracy = yes
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice
							is_female = yes
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = EMPEROR
						}
						AND = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = DUKE
						}
						AND = { # Ayatollah
							is_female = no
							religion = shiite
							tier = COUNT
						}
						AND = { # Évêque
							religion_group = christian
							tier = BARON
							NOT = { 
								has_minor_title = title_cardinal
								has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
							}
						}
						AND = { # Ervad
							religion = zoroastrian
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements tribaux
					is_tribal = yes
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
							is_female = yes
							tier = EMPEROR

								culture_group = altaic
								culture_group = dravidian_group
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group
								culture = russian
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
							spouse = {
								is_female = no
								real_tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { # sauf quand:
									culture_group = altaic
									culture_group = dravidian_group
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group
									culture = russian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no

						is_married = no

		localisation_key = String_FR_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			OR = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
				AND = { # gouvernements féodaux

					OR = {
						AND = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
							NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne

							tier = KING
							culture_group = byzantine

							NOT = { spouse = { real_tier = EMPEROR } } # conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire

							real_tier = DUKE
							OR = {
								liege = { culture_group = arabic } # Émir Émira

									culture = sogdian

								}

						}
						AND = { # Earl
							real_tier = COUNT
							is_female = no
							OR = {
								culture = saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
							NOT = {
								spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = COUNT } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
								liege = {
									NOR = {
										culture = saxon # Earl
										culture = english # Earl
										culture = scottish # Earl
										culture = irish # Earl
										culture = pictish # Earl
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = BARON
							is_female = no
							culture_group = iranian # Argbadh
							NOT = { spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON } } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						}
						AND = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
								NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
									culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
									culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
									culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
									culture = nahuatl # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani
									culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
									culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
									culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
									culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
									culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									AND = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
										OR = {
											culture = turkish # Padishah
											culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
											culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										}
										is_female = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Exarque)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = KING
							}
							spouse = {
								tier = KING
								primary_title = { is_vice_royalty = yes }
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = byzantine
									}
									liege = { culture_group = byzantine }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = DUKE
								OR = {
									AND = { # Émir Émira
										independent = yes
										culture_group = arabic

									liege = { culture_group = arabic } # Émir Émira
									AND = { # Ikhshide
										is_female = yes

										is_female = yes

										is_female = no
										liege = { culture_group = iranian }
									}
								}

						}

							is_female = no
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								tier = BARON

							spouse = {
								real_tier = COUNT

									AND = {
										independent = yes

											culture = saxon

											culture = scottish
											culture = irish
											culture = pictish
										}
									}

							is_ruler = no
							is_female = no
							spouse = {
								real_tier = BARON
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes

								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements théocratiques
					is_theocracy = yes
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice
							is_female = yes
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = EMPEROR
						}
						AND = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = DUKE
						}
						AND = { # Ayatollah
							is_female = no
							religion = shiite
							tier = COUNT
						}
						AND = { # Évêque
							religion_group = christian
							tier = BARON
							NOT = { 
								has_minor_title = title_cardinal
								has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
							}
						}
						AND = { # Ervad
							religion = zoroastrian
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements tribaux
					is_tribal = yes
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
							is_female = yes
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { # sauf quand:
								culture_group = altaic
								culture_group = dravidian_group
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group
								culture = russian
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
							spouse = {
								is_female = no
								real_tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { # sauf quand:
									culture_group = altaic
									culture_group = dravidian_group
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group
									culture = russian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		localisation_key = String_FR_le_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no

		localisation_key = String_FR_L

							tier = KING

							real_tier = DUKE

								culture = saxon # Earl

								culture = scottish # Earl

								culture = pictish # Earl

							NOT = {
								spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = COUNT } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte

										culture = saxon # Earl
										culture = english # Earl
										culture = scottish # Earl

										culture = pictish # Earl
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = BARON
							is_female = no
							culture_group = iranian # Argbadh
							NOT = { spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON } } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						}
						AND = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
								NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
									culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
									culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
									culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
									culture = nahuatl # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani
									culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
									culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
									culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
									culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
									culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									AND = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
										OR = {
											culture = turkish # Padishah
											culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
											culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										}
										is_female = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Exarque)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = KING
							}
							spouse = {
								tier = KING
								primary_title = { is_vice_royalty = yes }
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = byzantine
									}
									liege = { culture_group = byzantine }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = DUKE
								OR = {
									AND = { # Émir Émira
										independent = yes

										is_female = no
										liege = { culture_group = iranian }

								is_ruler = no

								real_tier = COUNT

										independent = yes

							is_female = no

								real_tier = BARON
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes

								}
							}
						}
					}
				}

					is_theocracy = yes
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice
							is_female = yes
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = EMPEROR
						}
						AND = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = DUKE
						}
						AND = { # Ayatollah
							is_female = no
							religion = shiite
							tier = COUNT
						}
						AND = { # Évêque
							religion_group = christian
							tier = BARON
							NOT = { 
								has_minor_title = title_cardinal
								has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
							}
						}
						AND = { # Ervad
							religion = zoroastrian
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements tribaux
					is_tribal = yes
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
							is_female = yes
							tier = EMPEROR

								culture_group = altaic
								culture_group = dravidian_group
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group
								culture = russian
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
							spouse = {
								is_female = no
								real_tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { # sauf quand:
									culture_group = altaic
									culture_group = dravidian_group
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group
									culture = russian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...

					AND = {

					OR = {
						spouse = { is_landed = no }
						is_married = no

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			OR = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
				AND = { # gouvernements féodaux

					OR = {
						AND = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
							NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne

								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu

							tier = KING
							culture_group = byzantine

							NOT = { spouse = { real_tier = EMPEROR } } # conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						}

							real_tier = DUKE
							OR = {
								liege = { culture_group = arabic } # Émir Émira

									culture = sogdian
									is_female = no
								}

						}
						AND = { # Earl
							real_tier = COUNT
							is_female = no
							OR = {
								culture = saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
							NOT = {
								spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = COUNT } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
								liege = {
									NOR = {
										culture = saxon # Earl
										culture = english # Earl
										culture = scottish # Earl
										culture = irish # Earl
										culture = pictish # Earl
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = BARON
							is_female = no
							culture_group = iranian # Argbadh
							NOT = { spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON } } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						}
						AND = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
								NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
									culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
									culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
									culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
									culture = nahuatl # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani
									culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
									culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
									culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
									culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
									culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									AND = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
										OR = {
											culture = turkish # Padishah
											culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
											culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										}
										is_female = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Exarque)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = KING
							}
							spouse = {
								tier = KING
								primary_title = { is_vice_royalty = yes }
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = byzantine
									}
									liege = { culture_group = byzantine }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = DUKE
								OR = {
									AND = { # Émir Émira
										independent = yes
										culture_group = arabic
									}
									liege = { culture_group = arabic } # Émir Émira
									AND = { # Ikhshide
										is_female = yes
										independent = yes
										culture = sogdian
									}

										is_female = yes
										liege = { culture = sogdian }

										is_female = no
										independent = yes
										culture_group = iranian
									}
									AND = { # Émira
										is_female = no
										liege = { culture_group = iranian }

								}

						}

							is_female = no
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								tier = BARON
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = COUNT
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										OR = {
											culture = saxon
											culture = english
											culture = scottish
											culture = irish
											culture = pictish
										}

										OR = {
											culture = saxon
											culture = english
											culture = scottish
											culture = irish
											culture = pictish
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
							is_ruler = no
							is_female = no
							spouse = {
								real_tier = BARON
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = iranian
									}
									liege = { culture_group = iranian }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements théocratiques
					is_theocracy = yes
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice
							is_female = yes
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = EMPEROR
						}
						AND = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = DUKE
						}
						AND = { # Ayatollah
							is_female = no
							religion = shiite
							tier = COUNT
						}
						AND = { # Évêque
							religion_group = christian
							tier = BARON
							NOT = { 
								has_minor_title = title_cardinal
								has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
							}
						}
						AND = { # Ervad
							religion = zoroastrian
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements tribaux
					is_tribal = yes
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
							is_female = yes
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { # sauf quand:
								culture_group = altaic
								culture_group = dravidian_group
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group
								culture = russian
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
							spouse = {
								is_female = no
								real_tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { # sauf quand:
									culture_group = altaic
									culture_group = dravidian_group
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group
									culture = russian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_au_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}

		localisation_key = String_FR_a_la_

				AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...

						is_tribal = yes
					}

				}
				spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
					AND = { 
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur

					OR = {
						spouse = { is_landed = no }
						is_married = no

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_A_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			OR = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
				AND = { # gouvernements féodaux
					is_feudal = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
							NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne

								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu

							tier = KING
							culture_group = byzantine

							NOT = { spouse = { real_tier = EMPEROR } } # conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = DUKE
							OR = {
								liege = { culture_group = arabic } # Émir Émira

									culture = sogdian
									is_female = no
								}

						}
						AND = { # Earl
							real_tier = COUNT
							is_female = no
							OR = {
								culture = saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
							NOT = {
								spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = COUNT } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
								liege = {
									NOR = {
										culture = saxon # Earl
										culture = english # Earl
										culture = scottish # Earl
										culture = irish # Earl
										culture = pictish # Earl
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = BARON
							is_female = no
							culture_group = iranian # Argbadh
							NOT = { spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON } } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						}
						AND = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
								NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
									culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
									culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
									culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
									culture = nahuatl # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani
									culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
									culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
									culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
									culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
									culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
									AND = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
										OR = {
											culture = turkish # Padishah
											culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
											culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										}
										is_female = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Exarque)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = KING
							}
							spouse = {
								tier = KING
								primary_title = { is_vice_royalty = yes }
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = byzantine
									}
									liege = { culture_group = byzantine }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = DUKE
								OR = {
									AND = { # Émir Émira
										independent = yes
										culture_group = arabic
									}
									liege = { culture_group = arabic } # Émir Émira
									AND = { # Ikhshide
										is_female = yes
										independent = yes
										culture = sogdian
									}
									AND = { # Ikhshide
										is_female = yes
										liege = { culture = sogdian }
									}
									AND = { # Émira
										is_female = no
										independent = yes
										culture_group = iranian
									}
									AND = { # Émira
										is_female = no
										liege = { culture_group = iranian }
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Earl)
							is_female = no
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								tier = BARON
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = COUNT
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										OR = {
											culture = saxon
											culture = english
											culture = scottish
											culture = irish
											culture = pictish
										}
									}
									liege = {
										OR = {
											culture = saxon
											culture = english
											culture = scottish
											culture = irish
											culture = pictish
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
							is_ruler = no
							is_female = no
							spouse = {
								real_tier = BARON
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes
										culture_group = iranian
									}
									liege = { culture_group = iranian }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements théocratiques
					is_theocracy = yes
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice
							is_female = yes
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = EMPEROR
						}
						AND = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = DUKE
						}
						AND = { # Ayatollah
							is_female = no
							religion = shiite
							tier = COUNT
						}
						AND = { # Évêque
							religion_group = christian
							tier = BARON
							NOT = { 
								has_minor_title = title_cardinal
								has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
							}
						}
						AND = { # Ervad
							religion = zoroastrian
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements tribaux
					is_tribal = yes
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
							is_female = yes
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { # sauf quand:
								culture_group = altaic
								culture_group = dravidian_group
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group
								culture = russian
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
							spouse = {
								is_female = no
								real_tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { # sauf quand:
									culture_group = altaic
									culture_group = dravidian_group
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group
									culture = russian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		localisation_key = String_FR_Au_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}

							real_tier = DUKE

								culture = saxon # Earl

								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
							NOT = {
								spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = COUNT } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte

									NOR = {
										culture = saxon # Earl
										culture = english # Earl
										culture = scottish # Earl
										culture = irish # Earl
										culture = pictish # Earl
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							real_tier = BARON
							is_female = no
							culture_group = iranian # Argbadh
							NOT = { spouse = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON } } # si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						}
						AND = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice
								NOT = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
									culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
									culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
									culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
									culture = nahuatl # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani
									culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
									culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin

									culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine

									AND = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
										OR = {
											culture = turkish # Padishah
											culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
											culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										}
										is_female = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Exarque)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = KING
							}
							spouse = {
								tier = KING
								primary_title = { is_vice_royalty = yes }
								OR = {
									AND = {
										independent = yes

									}
									liege = { culture_group = byzantine }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
							}
							spouse = {
								real_tier = DUKE

									AND = { # Émir Émira
										independent = yes

								real_tier = COUNT

										independent = yes

						AND = { # Impératrice
							is_female = yes
							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = EMPEROR
						}

							religion_group = pagan_group
							tier = DUKE
						}
						AND = { # Ayatollah
							is_female = no
							religion = shiite
							tier = COUNT
						}
						AND = { # Évêque
							religion_group = christian
							tier = BARON
							NOT = { 
								has_minor_title = title_cardinal
								has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
							}
						}
						AND = { # Ervad
							religion = zoroastrian
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # gouvernements tribaux
					is_tribal = yes
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
					OR = {
						AND = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
							is_female = yes
							tier = EMPEROR

								culture_group = altaic

								is_female = no
								real_tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { # sauf quand:
									culture_group = altaic
									culture_group = dravidian_group
									culture_group = indo_aryan_group
									culture = russian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

defined_text = {
	name = Get_only_le_SocietyRank
	use_first_valid = yes
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_l
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = secret_religious_cult
						society_member_of = monastic_order_benedictine
						society_member_of = monastic_order_dominican
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 2
					}
				}
				AND = {
					society_member_of = hermetics
					OR = {
						society_rank == 2
						society_rank == 3
					}
				}
				AND = {
					society_member_of = monastic_order_buddhist
					OR = {
						society_rank >= 3
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_hindu
						society_member_of = monastic_order_jain
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_monophysite
						society_member_of = monastic_order_nestorian
						society_member_of = monastic_order_orthodox
						society_member_of = the_assassins
						society_member_of = the_cold_ones
						society_member_of = the_satanists
						society_member_of = monastic_order_stoics # Étudiant, Étudiante
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 1
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = the_cult_of_kali
						society_member_of = the_plaguebringers
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 1
						society_rank == 3
					}
				}
				AND = {
					society_member_of = the_vodouns
					OR = {
						society_rank == 1
						society_rank == 4
					}
				}
				AND = { # Héroïne
					OR = {
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_norse
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_tengri
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_baltic
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_finnish
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_slavic
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_west_african
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_zun
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_bon
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_hellenic
					}
					society_rank == 4
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_le_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_la_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

						society_member_of = monastic_order_hindu
						society_member_of = monastic_order_jain
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_monophysite
						society_member_of = monastic_order_nestorian
						society_member_of = monastic_order_orthodox
						society_member_of = the_assassins
						society_member_of = the_cold_ones
						society_member_of = the_satanists
						society_member_of = monastic_order_stoics # Étudiant, Étudiante
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 1
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = the_cult_of_kali
						society_member_of = the_plaguebringers
					}
					OR = {
						society_rank == 1
						society_rank == 3
					}
				}
				AND = {
					society_member_of = the_vodouns
					OR = {
						society_rank == 1
						society_rank == 4
					}
				}
				AND = { # Héroïne
					OR = {
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_norse
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_tengri
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_baltic
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_finnish
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_slavic
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_west_african
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_zun
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_bon
						society_member_of = warrior_lodge_hellenic
					}
					society_rank == 4
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
	}
}

					has_job_title = job_chancellor
					liege = {
						NOT = { 
							religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Astabadh
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_job_title = job_marshal
					liege = {
						NOT = { 
							religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Eran Spahbod
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_job_title = job_treasurer
					liege = {
						OR = {
							culture = greek # Sacellaire
							religion = aztec # Petlacalcatl
							culture = bodpa # Gnyer
							culture = han # Trésorier
							culture = jurchen # Trésorier
							culture = tangut # Gnyer
							religion = taoist # Trésorier
							religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Darik-pat
						}
					}
				}
				has_job_title = job_spymaster
				AND = {
					has_job_title = job_spiritual
					liege = {
						NOT = {
							religion_group = indian_group # Upadhyaya
							AND = {
								religion_group = muslim # Imam de la Cour
								NOT = { religion = shiite } # Mollah de la Cour
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_job_title = job_chancellor
					liege = {
						OR = {
							culture = bodpa # Lönchen
							culture = tangut # Lönchen
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_job_title = job_spiritual
					liege = {
						OR = {
							culture = bodpa # Banchenmo
							religion = norse_pagan # Voyante
							religion = norse_pagan_reformed # Voyante
							culture = tangut # Banchenmo
							religion_group = indian_group # Upadhyaya
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_job_title = job_treasurer
					liege = {
						OR = {
						culture = bodpa # Gnyer
						culture = tangut # Gnyer
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_APOSTROPHE
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { # femmes
					is_female = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_spiritual
							liege = {
								OR = {
									religion_group = indian_group # Upadhyaya
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { # hommes
					is_female = no
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_chancellor
							liege = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group } # Astabadh
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_marshal
							liege = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group } # Eran Spahbod
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_treasurer
							NOT = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = greek # Sacellaire
										religion = aztec # Petlacalcatl
										culture = bodpa # Gnyer
										culture = han # Trésorier
										culture = jurchen # Trésorier
										culture = tangut # Gnyer
										religion = taoist # Trésorier
										religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Darik-pat
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_job_title = job_spiritual
							liege = {
								OR = {
									religion_group = indian_group # Upadhyaya
									AND = {
										religion_group = muslim # Imam de la Cour
										NOT = { religion = shiite } # Mollah de la Cour
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = Get_only_du_HighGod
	use_first_valid = yes
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					religion = aztec
					aztec = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = aztec_reformed
					aztec_reformed = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = baltic_pagan
					baltic_pagan = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = baltic_pagan_reformed
					baltic_pagan_reformed = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = bogomilist
					bogomilist = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = bon
					bon = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = bon_reformed
					bon_reformed = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = buddhist
					buddhist = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = cathar
					cathar = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = catholic
					catholic = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = druze
					druze = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = finnish_pagan
					finnish_pagan = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}
				AND = {
					religion = finnish_pagan_reformed
					finnish_pagan_reformed = { is_name_randomized = yes }	
				}

## CUSTOM ENGLISH COMMANDS WITH ARTICLE OR GENDER

defined_text = {
	name = GetCapitalHoldingDuDela # Returns a suitable name for the main building of your capital
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_FALLBACK_GetCapitalHoldingDuDela
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Castle_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = castle	}
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Castle_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = castle	}
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = KING }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Castle_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = castle	}
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Temple_1
		trigger = { capital_holding = { holding_type = temple	} }
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Nomad_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = nomad }
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Nomad_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = nomad }
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = KING }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Nomad_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = nomad }
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Tribal_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = tribal	}
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Tribal_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = tribal	}
			higher_tier_than = COUNT
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Tribal_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = tribal	}
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_City_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = city }
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_City_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = city }
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = KING }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_City_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = city }
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetHoldingDuDela_Fallback_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				capital_holding = {
					OR = {
						holding_type = castle
						holding_type = temple
						holding_type = nomad
						holding_type = tribal
						holding_type = city
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
